2. Attentive service: Maybe because I stayed for two days, the front desk upgraded me to a deluxe twin room and gave me a small Spring Festival gift box. 3. The room is comfortable: the room is large, the bed is big enough, clean and tidy. Smart toilet seats are winter-friendly. I live on the 12th floor and look out at the small garden in front of the hotel. Opposite is Wanda Plaza. There are green mountains in the distance. The view is wide. The sunset in the evening adds to the window view. I can see fireworks blooming from time to time at night, which is great.
4. Special recommendation: The breakfast is rich, the buffet dinner is also good, the dishes are rich, and it is worth the price; during the Spring Festival, there is a lion dance performance presented by Cai Lifu Boxing and Martial Arts School in the morning, which is very exciting and can be enjoyed by all ages.
